Z3 branch: lcube
Z3 options: "-T:60 smt.random_seed=700 lp.lcube=true"
Z3 inputs: inputs/QF_NIA_small
Z3 commit message: Fix signed-overflow UB in mpz_manager::hash for INT_MIN

UBSan flagged `::abs(a.m_val)` at mpz.cpp:1908 as undefined behavior when
a.m_val == INT_MIN (negation overflows int). Compute the absolute value in
unsigned arithmetic instead; hash values are unchanged for all other inputs.

Surfaced while running ASan/UBSan on QF_NIA benchmarks in the polynomial
hashing hot path.

Co-authored-by: Copilot <223556219+Copilot@users.noreply.github.com>
